function showChat(currentPageUrl, chatRootRelativePath){
  chatRootRelativePath = chatRootRelativePath.replace(/\//g, '\/');
  currentPageUrl = currentPageUrl.replace(/\//g, '\/');
  if(currentPageUrl.indexOf(chatRootRelativePath)>0){
    // url matches, show chat
    return true;
  }
  // dont show chat
  return false;
}

function lastUrlPart(fullUrlStr, comparisonUrlPartStr, comparisonUrlFullStr) {
    /* check if url ends with certain string plus matched base url too. Remove ending slash from tested url, before comparison is done */
     if(fullUrlStr.length > 0){
        fullUrlStr = fullUrlStr.toLowerCase();
        if(fullUrlStr.charAt(fullUrlStr.length-1)=='/'){
          //strip ending slash, if exists:
          fullUrlStr = fullUrlStr.substring(0, fullUrlStr.length - 1);
        }
        var validatedUrlStr = fullUrlStr.substring(fullUrlStr.lastIndexOf("/")+1); 
        if((validatedUrlStr == comparisonUrlPartStr) && (fullUrlStr.indexOf(comparisonUrlFullStr)!=-1)){
          return "yes";
        }
    }
    //no matches between fullUrlStr and comparisonUrlPartStr
    return "no";
}

  <script>
   if(helFiChat_localization && helFiChat_variant == 'new'){
var _genesys = {
    onReady: [],
    chat: {
        registration: false,
        localization : helFiChat_localization,
        onReady: [],
        ui: {
            onBeforeChat: function (chat) {              
                setTimeout(function(){
                windowWidth = $(window).width();
                windowHeight = $(window).height();
                bodyHeight = windowHeight - 50;
                if (windowWidth <= 575) {
	        $('.gwc-chat-body').height(bodyHeight);                 
                } else if (windowHeight <= 425) {                   
	        $('.gwc-chat-body').height(bodyHeight);
                }
                                 
                var headElement = '.gwc-chat-head';
                var text = helFiChat_title_temp;                                       
                jQuery(headElement).find('.gwc-chat-title').replaceWith('<h2 class="gwc-chat-title">' + text +  '</h2>');
                $('.gwc-chat-head').prepend($( '.gwc-chat-logo' ));
                $('.gwc-chat-logo').replaceWith($('.gwc-chat-logo-helsinki'));
                $('.gwc-chat-branding').remove();
                $('#chatAuthenticationElement').clone().prependTo('.gwc-chat-body');
                if($('#chatAuthenticationElement').css('display') == 'flex') {                       
                        $('div.gwc-chat-message-container').css("top", "100px");                      
                        } else {                      
                        $('div.gwc-chat-message-container').css('top', '63px');                       
                        }                                                                                                       
                $('#preload').append('<img class="gwc-chat-logo-helsinki" tabindex="0" title="helsinki-logo" alt="helsinki-logo" src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/project-logo-hki-white-fi.png"/>');                                          
                $( '.gwc-chat-icon-close' ).replaceWith($('.gwc-chat-icon-iks'));                
                $('#preload').append('<img class="gwc-chat-icon-iks" onkeypress="onEnter(event, this)" tabindex="0"' + helfiChat_close + 'src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/close-next.svg" />');                     
                $( '.gwc-chat-icon-minimize' ).replaceWith($('.gwc-chat-icon-down'));
                $('#preload').append('<img id="minimize" onclick="toggleFlip()" onkeypress="onEnter(event, this)" class="gwc-chat-icon-down"  tabindex="0"' + helfiChat_minimize + 'src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/arrow_down.svg" />');
                $('.gwc-chat-message-form').append($('.gwc-chat-btn'));
                $('#preload').append('<input class="gwc-chat-btn" onkeypress="onEnter(event, this)"  tabindex="0" type="image"' + helfiChat_send + 'src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/arrow_black.svg" />');                           
                $("textarea").attr({rows:"1", placeholder:helfiChat_placeholder}); 
                $("textarea").attr("tabindex", "0");
                $("textarea").attr("onfocusout", "addFocus()");
                $("textarea").attr("onclick", "removeFocus()");
                $("textarea").attr("aria-label", helfiChat_message);
                 element = document.getElementsByClassName("gwc-chat-embedded-window")[0];
                 element.setAttribute('role', 'region');
		             element.setAttribute('aria-roledescription', text);   
                 document.getElementsByClassName("gwc-persistent-chat-messages")[0].setAttribute('aria-live', 'polite');                           
                }, 0);                                                   
                 
                _genesys.chat.onReady.push(function (chatWidgetApi) {                  
                    chatWidgetApi.restoreChat({                   
                        serverUrl: helFiChat_serverUrl,
                        registration: function (done) {
                            done({
                                 service:helFiChat_service,Language:helFiChat_language,                  
                            });
                        }
                    }).done(function (session) {                                                                                                  
                        session.setUserData({
                           service:helFiChat_service,Language:helFiChat_language,                          
                        });                      
                        $('.gwc-chat-btn').on("click", function(){
                           var text = $('textarea.gwc-chat-input').val();
                           session.sendMessage(text);
                           $('textarea.gwc-chat-input').val('').focus();                      
                        });                     
                        session.onMessageReceived(function(event) {
                        $( ".gwc-chat-message-time" ).last().html( function(){
                        var time = $(this).html().slice(1, -4);
                        $(this).html(time);                                                              
                        })                                                     
                        if (event.party.type.client) {
                         $(".gwc-chat-message-author").last().siblings( ".gwc-chat-message-text" ).attr('id', 'user-message').removeClass( "gwc-chat-message-text" );
                          //helfiChatAuthorUser();
                          $("div#user-message").prev().css({"text-align": "right", "display": "block", "color": "grey", "font-size": "12px"});
                          $( ".gwc-chat-message-time" ).last().appendTo($("div#user-message").last());
                          $('.gwc-chat-message').last().append('<img class="gwc-chat-head-icon" src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/user_black.svg"' + helfiChat_user + '/>');                                               
                          var link = $("div#user-message").last().html().replace(/((([A-Za-z]{3,9}:(?:\/\/)?)(?:[\-;:&=\+\$,\w]+@)?[A-Za-z0-9\.\-]+|(?:www\.|[\-;:&=\+\$,\w]+@)[A-Za-z0-9\.\-]+)((?:\/[\+~%\/\.\w\-_]*)?\??(?:[\-\+=&;%@\.\w_]*)#?(?:[\.\!\/\\\w]*))?)/g, '<a href="$1" target="_blank">$1</a>');                            
                          $("div#user-message").last().html(link);
                          } else {                       
                          $( ".gwc-chat-message-time" ).last().appendTo($("div.gwc-chat-message-text").last());                                                    
                          $('.gwc-chat-message').last().prepend($('#preload').find('.gwc-chat-head-icon'));
                          $('#preload').append('<img class="gwc-chat-head-icon" style="width:35px !important; height:40px !important;" src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/agent_blue.svg"' + helfiChat_agent + '/>');                         
                         $(".gwc-chat-message-author").last().siblings( ".gwc-chat-message-text" ).each(function(){if($(this).text().trim().length < 6){$(this)[0].parentElement.remove();}}); 
//helfiChatAuthorAgent();
                          }
                        }); 
                        session.onSessionEnded(function() {                              
                            $("textarea").attr("disabled", "true"); 
                            $( ".gwc-chat-btn" ).remove();  
                          });                                   
                    }).fail(function (par) {
                        alert(par.description);
                    });
                });
            }
        }
    }
};
_genesys.cobrowse = false;
} //helFiChat_localization
  </script>
  <script language="javascript">
   function initHelFiChatLocalization_new() {
if(helFiChat_localization && helFiChat_variant == 'new'){
  //preload icons for chat
  $('#preload').append('<img class="gwc-chat-logo-helsinki" tabindex="0" title="helsinki-logo" alt="helsinki-logo" src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/project-logo-hki-white-fi.png"/>'); 
  $('#preload').append('<img class="gwc-chat-icon-iks" onkeypress="onEnter(event, this)" tabindex="0"' + helfiChat_close + 'src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/close-next.svg" />');  
  $('#preload').append('<img id="minimize" onclick="toggleFlip()" onkeypress="onEnter(event, this)" class="gwc-chat-icon-down"  tabindex="0"' + helfiChat_minimize + 'src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/arrow_down.svg" />');  
  $('#preload').append('<input class="gwc-chat-btn" onkeypress="onEnter(event, this)"  tabindex="0" type="image"' + helfiChat_send + 'src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/arrow_black.svg" />');
  $('#preload').append('<img class="gwc-chat-head-icon" style="width:35px !important; height:40px !important;" src="https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/agent_blue.svg"' + helfiChat_agent + '/>');
  var win = $(this);
  //after page has been loaded, initialize chat:
  setTimeout(function(){
  var elem = document.getElementsByClassName("gcb-startChat")[0];
  elem.setAttribute('tabindex', '0');
  elem.setAttribute('onkeypress', 'onEnter(event, this)');
  elem.setAttribute('role', 'button');
  if (win.width() <= 575 || win.height() <= 425) {
   if (helFiChat_button.indexOf('open')>0) {
   	helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/mobile_open1.svg" ) !important';   
     } else if (helFiChat_button.indexOf('busy')>0) {
      helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/mobile_busy1.svg" ) !important';
     } else {
      helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/mobile_closed_strike1.svg" ) !important';
     }
if(helfiChat_lang == "fi") {
  elem.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Chatin käynnistyspainike');
} else if (helfiChat_lang == "sv") {
  elem.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Chat startknapp');
} else {
  elem.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Chat Start-button');
}
  } else { 
	if (helfiChat_lang == "en") {
		elem.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Open chat');
		if (helFiChat_button.indexOf('open')>0){
			helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/chat-open-en.png" ) !important';
			elem.setAttribute('alt', 'Chat open');
            elem.setAttribute('title', 'Chat open');
		} else if (helFiChat_button.indexOf('busy')>0) {
    		helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/chat-busy-en.png" ) !important';
    		elem.setAttribute('alt', 'Queue in the chat');
            elem.setAttribute('title', 'Queue in the chat');
   		} else {
    		helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/chat-closed-en.png" ) !important';
    		elem.setAttribute('alt', 'Chat Closed');
        	elem.setAttribute('title', 'Chat Closed');
    	}
    } else if (helfiChat_lang == "sv"){
                elem.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Starta chatten');
		if (helFiChat_button.indexOf('open')>0){
			helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/chat-open-sv.png" ) !important';
                elem.setAttribute('alt', 'Chatten öppen');
        	elem.setAttribute('title', 'Chatten öppen');
		} else if (helFiChat_button.indexOf('busy')>0) {
    		helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/chat-busy-sv.png" ) !important';
                elem.setAttribute('alt', 'Kö i chatten');
        	elem.setAttribute('title', 'Kö i chatten');
   		} else {
    		helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/chat-closed-sv.png" ) !important';
                elem.setAttribute('alt', 'Chatten stängd');
        	elem.setAttribute('title', 'Chatten stängd');
        }  	
    } else {
    	if (helfiChat_lang == "fi") {
    		elem.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Avaa chat');
    		if (helFiChat_button.indexOf('open')>0){
                        helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/chat-open.png" ) !important';		
			elem.setAttribute('alt', 'Chatti avoinna');
	    		elem.setAttribute('title', 'Chatti avoinna');
		} else if (helFiChat_button.indexOf('busy')>0) {    	
                           helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/chat-busy.png" ) !important';
	    		  elem.setAttribute('alt', 'Jonoa chätissä');
        		  elem.setAttribute('title', 'Jonoa chätissä');
	   	} else {
                            helFiChat_button = 'background-image: url( "https://www.hel.fi/static/helsinki/chat/chat-closed.png" ) !important';	
	    		    elem.setAttribute('alt', 'Chatti suljettu');
        		    elem.setAttribute('title', 'Chatti suljettu');
	        }
	    }	  	
    }
}
if (document.getElementsByClassName("gwc-chat-embedded-window").length != 1){
  elem.setAttribute( 'style', helFiChat_button);

  //hide closed chat button for main page urls only:
  if(helFiChatPageUrl.toLowerCase() === 'https://www.hel.fi/helsinki/fi' || helFiChatPageUrl.toLowerCase() === 'https://www.hel.fi/helsinki/fi/' || helFiChatPageUrl.toLowerCase() === 'https://www.hel.fi/helsinki/sv' || helFiChatPageUrl.toLowerCase() === 'https://www.hel.fi/helsinki/sv/' || helFiChatPageUrl.toLowerCase() === 'https://www.hel.fi/helsinki/en' || helFiChatPageUrl.toLowerCase() === 'https://www.hel.fi/helsinki/en/'){
  if(helFiChat_button.indexOf('chat-closed')> -1 || helFiChat_button.indexOf('mobile_closed')> -1){
     //if chat closed, hide chat button:
     helFiChat_button = '';
     if(document.getElementsByClassName('gcb-startChat')[0] !== null){
       document.getElementsByClassName('gcb-startChat')[0].style.display = 'none';
     }
  } //chat-closed
 } //hide closed chat button for main page urls only

} else { 
console.log('CHAT ELEMENT NOT LOADED');
	}
  }, 1000);
 } // if chat == new
} //initHelFiChatLocalization

if(helFiChat_localization && helFiChat_variant == 'new'){
  window.addEventListener('load', initHelFiChatLocalization_new);
} //helFiChat_localization

if(helFiChat_localization && helFiChat_variant == 'new'){    
  $(window).on('resize', function() {
      var win = $(this);
      bodyHeight = win.height() - 50;
       if (win.width() <= 575) {
	        $('.gwc-chat-body').height(bodyHeight);                
       } else if (win.height() <= 425) {                   
	        $('.gwc-chat-body').height(bodyHeight);               
       }                       
});
}

function toggleFlip() {
   document.getElementsByClassName('gwc-chat-icon-down')[1].classList.toggle("flip");
   $('.gwc-chat-icon-down').attr('aria-label', function(index, attr){  
    return attr == arrowDownLabel ? arrowUpLabel : arrowDownLabel;
});
}

function onEnter(e, el) {
   if (e.keyCode === 13) {    
    el.click();
  }
}

function addFocus() { 
  $('textarea.gwc-chat-input').css('outline', '');  
} 
    
function removeFocus() {  
  $('textarea.gwc-chat-input').css('outline', 'unset'); 
}
  </script>

          <div class="highlight-text-content col-sm-6">
           <div class="highlight-title">
            <h2 class="news-title">
             <a href="/uutiset/fi/kaupunginkanslia/helsinki-varautuu-koronavirukseen-monin-tavoin" id="specialNewsItem">
              Ajankohtaista: Helsinki ja korona – toimi näin, jos epäilet saaneesi koronavirustartunnan
             </a>
            </h2>
            <span class="highlight-date timestamp">
             23.03.2020 18:45
            </span>
           </div>
           <p class="highlight-content standfirst">
            Kaupungin koronasivustolta löydät ajankohtaiset aiheet liittyen koronavirukseen. Helsinki tiedottaa kaupungin nettisivuilla ajankohtaisista muutoksista, linjauksista, ohjeistuksista sekä suosituksista.
           </p>
           <ul>
            <li>
             <a href="/sote/koronarokotus-fi" target="" title="Koronarokotukset">
              Koronarokotukset
             </a>
             <br/>
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="/helsinki/korona-fi/koronaneuvonta/voimassa-olevat-suositukset-ja-rajoitukset" target="" title="Voimassa olevat suositukset ja rajoitukset">
              Voimassa olevat suositukset ja rajoitukset
             </a>
             <br/>
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="/helsinki/korona-fi/koronaneuvonta/kasvomaskit/kaytto" target="" title="Kasvomaskien jakelu ja käyttö">
              Kasvomaskien jakelu ja käyttö
             </a>
             <br/>
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="/helsinki/korona-fi/sote-palvelut/korona-tilanne" target="" title="Helsingin koronavirustilannekatsaus">
              Helsingin koronavirustilannekatsaus
             </a>
             <br/>
            </li>
           </ul>

                  Kaikkea kivaa koululaisille ensi syksynä - iltapäivätoiminnan haku käynnistyy 22.3.
                 </a>
                </h1>
                <span class="news-carousel-date timestamp">
                 22.03.2021 06:45
                </span>
               </div>
               <p>
                Nyt on aika hakea koululaisten iltapäivätoimintaan. Iltapäivätoimintaan voivat hakea 1.-2. luokkalaiset sekä ylempien luokkien erityisen tuen oppilaat. Kaupunki toteuttaa toiminnan yhdessä järjestöjen, seurakuntien ja yksityisten palveluntuottajien kanssa. Hakuaika lukuvuoden 2021-2022 koululaisten iltapäivätoimintaan on 22.3.- 23.4.2021.
               </p>

                 </a>
                </h1>
                <span class="news-carousel-date timestamp">
                 19.03.2021 14:41
                </span>
               </div>
               <p>
                Kalasatamasta Pasilaan -hanke esittelee Pasilan alueen ja Hermannin rantatien suunnitelmia verkossa järjestettävässä asukastilaisuudessa 25.3.2021 klo 17–19. Tilaisuus on jaettu kahteen osaan siten, että ensimmäisen tunnin aikana esitellään Pasilan alueen liikennesuunnitelmia ja katusuunnitelmaluonnoksia ja toisen tunnin aikana Hermannin rantatien katusuunnitelmaluonnoksia.

                 </a>
                </h1>
                <span class="news-carousel-date timestamp">
                 19.03.2021 11:00
                </span>
               </div>
               <p>
                Järjestyksessään kolmas Helsinki Symposium pureutuu kaupunkien rooliin murroksen keskellä niin kotimaisesta kuin kansainvälisestä perspektiivistä sekä haastaa keskustelemaan kaupunkien kyvystä ja kyvykkyyksistä pandemian jälkeisen yhteiskunnan rakentamisessa. Helsinki Symposium toteutetaan virtuaalisena ja kutsuvieraiden lisäksi kaikille kiinnostuneille avoimena tapahtumana 24. maaliskuuta kello 13–16.

                <h1 class="news-title">
                 <a href="/uutiset/fi/kaupunginkanslia/tilinpaatos-2020-helsingin-talous-pysyi-kriisin-keskella-tasapainossa">
                  Tilinpäätös 2020: Helsingin talous pysyi kriisin keskellä tasapainossa, mutta pandemia ja sote-uudistus haastavat tulevaisuuden näkymiä
                 </a>
                </h1>
                <span class="news-carousel-date timestamp">
                 18.03.2021 14:04
                </span>
               </div>
               <p>
                Helsingin vuoden 2020 tilinpäätöksen mukaan kaupunki investoi enemmän kuin edellisenä vuonna. Kaupungin talouden tasapaino toteutui vuonna 2020 talousarviota parempana. Toiminnan ja investointien rahavirta jäi vain 9 miljoonaa euroa negatiiviseksi huolimatta edellistä vuotta merkittävästi korkeammasta investointitasosta. Tulos ylitti talousarvion 234 miljoonalla eurolla.  Tähän vaikutti merkittävästi valtiolta saadut kertaluonteiset kompensaatiot koronapandemiasta aiheutuneisiin taloudellisiin menetyksiin.
               </p>

                  Laajasalontiestä puistokatu – katuremontti alkaa
                 </a>
                </h1>
                <span class="news-carousel-date timestamp">
                 18.03.2021 12:22
                </span>
               </div>
               <p>
                Laajasalontien suuri katutyö alkaa maaliskuun lopulla. Katu rakennetaan kaupunkibulevardiksi eli puistokaduksi Yliskyläntien ja Koirasaarentien välillä. Katuremontin tarkoitus on taata toimivat ja nykyistä monipuolisemmat liikenneyhteydet Laajasalon asukkaille, joiden määrä tulee lähes kaksinkertaistumaan 20 vuodessa.
               </p>

Syntymäpäiviensä kunniaksi HRI etsii kaikkien aikojen mielenkiintoisinta pääkaupunkiseudun avointa dataa hyödyntävää sovellusta.

      <!-- EVENT CALENDAR SEARCH STARTS -->
      <script>
       var lang = document.documentElement.lang;

    var langTexts = {
        fi: {
            title: "Helsingissä tapahtuu",
            buttonTitle: "HAE",
            inputText: "Hae tapahtumia",
            allEvents: "Kaikki tapahtumat",
        },
        en: {
            title: "Helsinki events",
            buttonTitle: "Search",
            inputText: "Search events",
            allEvents: "All events",
        },
        sv: {
            title: "På gång i Helsingfors",
            buttonTitle: "Sök",
            inputText: "Sök evenemang",
            allEvents: "Alla evenemang",
        }
    }

    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', (event) => {
        LoadTexts();
    });

    function LoadTexts() {
        //Add dynamic texts 
        var searchTitle = document.getElementById('search-title');
        var searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
        var searchBtn = document.getElementById('searchBtn');
        var allEvents = document.getElementById('allEvents');
        var tapahtumatHref = "https://tapahtumat.hel.fi/" + lang + "/events";
        //Set title text
        searchTitle.innerHTML = langTexts[lang].title;

        //Set input text params
        searchInput.placeholder = langTexts[lang].inputText;
        searchInput.setAttribute("aria-label", langTexts[lang].inputText)

        //Set input button text params;
        searchBtn.innerHTML = langTexts[lang].buttonTitle;
        searchBtn.setAttribute("aria-label", langTexts[lang].buttonTitle)

        //Set all events text
        allEvents.innerHTML = langTexts[lang].allEvents + " »";
        allEvents.setAttribute("href", tapahtumatHref);
    }

    function searchAndRedirect() {
        //Example of full URL to be redirected:
        //https://tapahtumat.hel.fi/fi/events?text=Mary Poppins - Maija Poppanen&searchOriginSiteId=1

        var inputValue = document.getElementById('searchInput').value;
        var baseUrl = "https://tapahtumat.hel.fi/" + lang + "/events?";
        var textQuery = "text=" + encodeURIComponent(inputValue);
        var searchOriginSiteIdQuery = "&searchOriginSiteId=1";
        var finalUrl = baseUrl + textQuery + searchOriginSiteIdQuery;

        //Redirect
        window.location.href = finalUrl;
    }
    function handleEnter(ele) {
    if(event.key === 'Enter') {
        searchAndRedirect();        
    }
}
      </script>
      <div class="two-col-left" id="searchBlock">
       <div class="two-col-left-wrapper container">

                    border: 2px solid #333;
                }

                #searchBlock #searchBtn {
                    width: 100%;
                    color: white !important;
                    padding: 5px;
                    margin: 0px;
                    height: 41px;
                    box-sizing: border-box;
                }

                @media (max-width: 767px) {
                    #searchBlock .date-sel-col {
                        margin-top: 15px;
                    }
                }

                #searchBlock .all-link {
                    font-size: 1.2rem;
                    font-weight: bold;
                }

                #searchBlock #jrange td a {
                    height: 35px !important;
                    width: 35px !important;
                    line-height: 22px !important;
                    font-weight: bold;
                }

                #searchBlock #jrange input {
                    width: 100%;
                }

                #searchBlock #jrange div {
                    font-size: 1.2rem;
                }
         </style>
         <div class="inner-container col-sm-12">
          <h2 id="search-title">
          </h2>
          <div class="dates" id="jrange">
           <div class="row">
            <div class="col-md-9 col-sm-12 col-xs-12 mt-1 mb-1">
             <input aria-label="" id="searchInput" onkeydown="handleEnter(this)" placeholder="" type="search" value=""/>

            <div class="col-md-3 col-md-offset-0 col-sm-6 col-sm-offset-6 col-xs-12 mt-1 mb-1">

               Helsinkiä rakennetaan vilkkaammin kuin koskaan. Kokonaisille uusille alueille tulee asuntoja, toimitiloja, päiväkoteja, kouluja, puistoja, ulkoilureittejä ja katuja.
              </p>
              <span aria-hidden="true">
               <a class="read-more" href="https://www.uuttahelsinkia.fi">
                Tutustu uusiin alueisiin »
               </a>
              </span>
             </div>

      <script>
       // Function that adds padding to bottom of image highlights so titles are aligned in case images are of different height
function padImages(){
  var images = $(".second-highlight-crop img");
  var height = 0;
  var tallestImage;
  for(var i = 0; i < images.length; i++){
    if(images[i].height > height){
      height = images[i].height;
      tallestImage = images[i];
    }
  }

  for(var i = 0; i < images.length; i++){
    images[i].style["padding-bottom"] = (height - images[i].height) + "px";
  }
};
$(window).on( 'load', padImages);
$(window).on( 'resize', padImages);
      </script>

      <script>
       /* corona green wave special highlight formatting */
if (document.getElementsByClassName('highlight-content').length > 0){
  //document.getElementsByClassName('highlight-content')[0].style.display = 'none';
}

if (document.getElementsByClassName('read-more').length > 0){
  document.getElementsByClassName('read-more')[0].style.display = 'none';
}

if (document.getElementsByClassName('highlight-date').length > 0){
  document.getElementsByClassName('highlight-date')[0].style.display = 'none';
}

if (document.getElementsByClassName('news-title').length > 0){
//uutiset/fi/kaupunginkanslia/helsinki-varautuu-koronavirukseen-monin-tavoin
 if(document.getElementsByClassName('news-title')[0].innerHTML.indexOf('koronavirus') || document.getElementsByClassName('news-title')[0].innerHTML.indexOf('corona') || document.getElementsByClassName('news-title')[0].innerHTML.indexOf('covid')){
  document.getElementsByClassName('news-title')[0].innerHTML = document.getElementsByClassName('news-title')[0].innerHTML.replace('uutiset/fi/kaupunginkanslia/helsinki-varautuu-koronavirukseen-monin-tavoin','helsinki/korona-fi/');
  document.getElementsByClassName('news-title')[0].style.textDecoration = "underline"; 
 }
}

/* special static copy green wave link handling: */
if(document.getElementById('specialNewsItem') !=null){
  if(document.getElementById('specialNewsItem').href != null){
      if(document.getElementById('specialNewsItem').href.indexOf('portal')>-1){
         if(document.getElementById('specialNewsItem').href.indexOf('-fi')>-1){
            document.getElementById('specialNewsItem').href = 'https://www.hel.fi/static/mirror-v2/archive/www.hel.fi/helsinki/korona-fi/'; 
        }
      }
  }
}
      </script>

            <span aria-live="polite" class="ui-helper-hidden-accessible" role="status">
            </span>
            <input aria-label="Hae yhteystietoja" autocomplete="off" class="search-input ui-autocomplete-input order-1" id="query" name="query" placeholder="Hae yhteystietoja" style="width:230px; height:30px;" tabindex="" type="text"/>

         <script>
          document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(event) {
	var $searchForm2 = $( '#search-form2' );
	if ($searchForm2){
	
		var url = $searchForm2.attr('action').replace('query-meta','velocity');
		var $searchField2 = $searchForm2.find('#query');
		var dictionary = $searchForm2.find('#search-dictionary').val();
			
		$searchField2.autocomplete({
			source: function(request, response) {
	    		$.getJSON(url, { 
	                          'v.app': 'autocomplete-json',
	                          'v.function':'autocomplete-collection', 
	                          'bag-of-words': true, 
	                          'num':10, 
	                          'filter': '', 
	                          'dictionary':dictionary,
	                          'str': request.term 
	                          }, function (data){
	                              var suggestions = data.suggestions ? data.suggestions.map(function (suggestion) { return suggestion.term; }) : [];
	                              response(suggestions);
	                          });
	  		},
	  		select: function (event, ui){
	  			if (ui.item.value){
	  				$searchField2.val(ui.item.value);
	  				$searchForm2.submit();
	  			}
	  		},
			minLength: 2
			
		});
		
	}
	
});
         </script>

     <!-- readspeaker webreader -->
     <script type="text/javascript">
      /* Custom ReadSpeakers Javascript created to fix issues with page links of ReadSpeaker
 * @language - language in which ReadSpeaker will say the text.
 * @hostName - hostname of the page which ReadSpeaker will read.
 * *@pageUrl - path of the page (without host).
 * @pageIdParameter - page ID parameter in the URL.
 * *@readspeaker-link - ReadSpeaker button element.
 * *@readspeaker-item-url - ReadSpeaker parameter for the full URL
 */
function setReadSpeakerParameters(){
	var defaultLanguage = "fi_fi";
	var defaultHostName = "https://www.hel.fi";
	var fullPath = "";
	var href = "https://app-eu.readspeaker.com/cgi-bin/rsent?customerid=4420";
	var onClick = "openAndRead('https://app-eu.readspeaker.com/cgi-bin/rsent?customerid=4420";
	
	// Appending language parameter if exists. Default: fi_fi
	if(elementByIdExists('language')){ 
		var language = document.getElementById('language').value;
		href += "&lang=" + language;
		onClick += "&lang=" + language;
	}else{
		href += "&lang=" + defaultLanguage;
		onClick += "&lang=" + defaultLanguage;
	}
	
	href += "&output=template";
	
	// Appending hostName parameter if exists. Default: https://www.hel.fi
	if(elementByIdExists('hostName')){
		var hostName = document.getElementById('hostName').value;
		href += "&url=" + hostName;
		onClick += "&url=" + hostName;
		fullPath += hostName;
	}else{
		href += "&url=" + defaultHostName;
		onClick += "&url=" + defaultHostName;
		fullPath += defaultHostName;
	}
	
	// Appending pageUrl parameter. If doesn't exist, script won't run!
	if(elementByIdExists('pageUrl')){
		var pageUrl = document.getElementById('pageUrl').value;
		href += pageUrl;
		onClick += pageUrl;
		fullPath += pageUrl;
	}else{
		console.log("Missing input with ID: pageUrl! Please add one in order to run script.");
	}
	
	// Appending pageIdParameter parameter if exists.
	if(elementByIdExists('pageIdParameter')){
		var pageIdParameter = document.getElementById('pageIdParameter').value;
		href += "%3fid%3d" + pageIdParameter;
		onClick += "%3fid%3d" + pageIdParameter;
		fullPath += "%3fid%3d" + pageIdParameter;
	}
	
	onClick += "'); return false;";
	
	// Setting href and onlick for readspeaker-link parameter. If doesn't exist, script won't run!
	if(elementByIdExists('readspeaker-link')){
		var linkElement = document.getElementById('readspeaker-link');
		linkElement.href = href;
		linkElement.setAttribute("onclick", onClick);
	}else{
		console.log("Missing ReadSpearker's link with ID: readspeaker-link! Please add one in order to run script.");
	}
	
	// Setting value for readspeaker-item-url input. If doesn't exist, script won't run!
	if(elementByIdExists('readspeaker-item-url')){
		var urlItem = document.getElementById('readspeaker-item-url');
		urlItem.value = fullPath;
		
	}else{
		console.log("Missing ReadSpearker's input with ID: readspeaker-item-url! Please add one in order to run script.");
	}
}

function elementByIdExists(parameterID){
	if(document.getElementById(parameterID) !== null){
		return true;
	}
	return false;
}

$( document ).ready(function() {
        // detect readspeaker v1 and v2 elements. If v2 elements present, do not run this v1-script:
	if(elementByIdExists('pageUrl') && elementByIdExists('readspeaker-link') && elementByIdExists('readspeaker-item-url') && !elementByIdExists('readspeaker_button1_link') && !elementByIdExists('readspeaker_button1_topnavi')){
		//setReadSpeakerParameters();
	}else{
		console.log("ReadSpeaker URL fix script disabled or v2 Readspeaker present.");
	}
});
     </script>
     <!-- READSPEAKER JS-LIBRARY v2: -->
     <script type="text/javascript">
      function parseAndPickFromList(parseRsList,parseRsListType){
 // Readspeaker readid or readclass input parameter validator and picker
    // Input: id or class html-element list separated by |. 
    // Seek if web page contains one, 
    // Output: return id or class name when first occurance happens
    var arrayRsElements = parseRsList.split('|');
    var arrayRsElementsLength = arrayRsElements.length;
    var testClassElement;
    var returnValueRs = false;
    for (var i = 0; i < arrayRsElementsLength; i++) {
      if(parseRsListType=="rsClass"){
        testClassElement = document.getElementsByClassName(arrayRsElements[i]);
        console.log('***' + parseRsListType+ '***' + arrayRsElements[i] + '=' + document.getElementsByClassName(arrayRsElements[i])[0] + '***' + testClassElement[0]);
        if(testClassElement[0]){
          returnValueRs=arrayRsElements[i];
          break;
        }
      }
      else if(parseRsListType=="rsId"){
        console.log('***' + parseRsListType+ '***' + arrayRsElements[i] + '=' + document.getElementById(arrayRsElements[i]));
       if(document.getElementById(arrayRsElements[i])){
         returnValueRs=arrayRsElements[i];
          break;
       }
      }
      else{
        console.log('parseAndPickFromList():parseRsListType error: RETURN FALSE');
       returnValueRs=false;
      }
    } //for loop
  console.log('parseAndPickFromList():return value:'+returnValueRs);
 return returnValueRs;
}

function setupReadSpeaker(rsReadClassList, rsReadIdList, rsLanguage, rsCurrentUrl, partialReplaceSource, partialReplaceWith){
/*
rsReadClassList - list of class-elements to search from page and to read. First occurence picked.
rsReadIdList - list of id-elements to search from page and to read. First occurence picked.
rsLanguage - fi, fi_fi, sv_se, etc
rsCurrentUrl - hel.fi portal page url to read
partialReplaceSource - optional. Replace default gui element read url parts having this string
partialReplaceWith - optional. Replace default gui element read url parts (partialReplaceSource) with this string
*/
var rsReadElement = '&readclass=main-content'; //default readelement

var rsLangElement = '&lang=fi_fi'; //default lang
//convert lang to readspeaker accepted format:
if(rsLanguage){
 if(rsLanguage=='fi') rsLanguage = 'fi_fi';
 if(rsLanguage=='sv') rsLanguage = 'sv_se';
 if(rsLanguage=='en') rsLanguage = 'en_uk';
 if(rsLanguage=='se') rsLanguage = 'sv_se';
 if(rsLanguage=='sv_sv') rsLanguage = 'sv_se';
 if(rsLanguage=='se_se') rsLanguage = 'sv_se';
 if(rsLanguage=='en_en') rsLanguage = 'en_uk';
}
 rsLangElement='&lang=' + rsLanguage;
//seek class read elements from html page:
if(rsReadClassList){
  rsReadClassList=parseAndPickFromList(rsReadClassList,'rsClass');
  if(rsReadClassList) rsReadElement='&readclass='+rsReadClassList;
}

//seek id read elements from html page:
if(rsReadIdList){
  rsReadIdList=parseAndPickFromList(rsReadIdList,'rsId');
  if(rsReadIdList) rsReadElement='&readid='+rsReadIdList;
}
// get also querystring part for readspeaker:
var queryStringPart = '';
var urlForRS = window.location.search;
if(urlForRS){
 if(urlForRS.indexOf('?') != -1){
    queryStringPart = window.location.search;
    queryStringPart = escape(queryStringPart);
  }
}
// if Readspeaker control gui found on page, continue starting readspeaker:
if(document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1') && document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1_link')){
  // turn readspeaker gui visible to page: 
  document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1').style.display = '';document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1').style.display = 'block';

  // default readspeaker integration, set up url to read/integrate with:
  if(!partialReplaceSource || !partialReplaceWith){
        document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1_link').href='https://app-eu.readspeaker.com/cgi-bin/rsent?customerid=4420' + rsLangElement + rsReadElement + '&url=' + rsCurrentUrl + queryStringPart;
    console.log('WCM: javascript-html: Readspeaker hel.fi url has been succesfullyset to:' + document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1_link').href);
   }
    else if(partialReplaceSource && partialReplaceWith){
        // Use readspeaker integration from its gui element, but replace string1 with string2 in it:
       document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1_link').href = document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1_link').href.replace( partialReplaceSource,partialReplaceWith);
    }
    else{
      // some readspeaker parameters are missing:
      console.log('WCM: javascript-html: Readspeaker hel.fi integration error: incorrect parameters');
      return false;
    }
  }
  else{
    // Error, Readspeaker control gui was not found on page:
      console.log('WCM: javascript-html: Readspeaker hel.fi integration error: cannot find readspeaker_button1 or readspeaker_button1_link -elements!');
    if(document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1_topnavi')){ 
      // disable listen button from header, since readspeaker cannot start:
      document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1_topnavi').style.display = '';
      document.getElementById('readspeaker_button1_topnavi').style.display = 'none';
    }
  }
  // all set up correctly for readspeaker:
  if(document.getElementsByClassName('rsplay')[0]){
    // start readspeaker directly from play-GUI:
    document.getElementsByClassName('rsplay')[0].click();
  }else{
    // cannot access rsplay -element on readspeaker gui:
    console.log('WCM: javascript-html: Readspeaker hel.fi integration error: class not found: rsplay');
  }
  return false;
}
     </script>

     <script language="javascript">
      var pageTitleThis = "";
  function twshareCurrentPage() {
    window.open("https://twitter.com/share?url=" + window.location.href + "&text=" + encodeURIComponent(pageTitleThis), '',
      'menubar=no,toolbar=no,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,height=300,width=600');
  }

function initHelFiTwitter() {
//after page has been loaded, initialize twitter sharing:
  pageTitleThis = document.getElementsByName('twitter:description')[0].getAttribute('content');
  if (!pageTitleThis) {
    pageTitleThis = document.getElementsByName('twitter:title')[0].getAttribute('content');
  } 
}
 
  function fbshareCurrentPage() {
    window.open("https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=" + escape(window.location.href) + "&t=" + document.title, '',
      'menubar=no,toolbar=no,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,height=300,width=600');
  }

window.addEventListener('load', initHelFiTwitter);
     </script>
